DECLARE @inserted32 TABLE ([Id] int, [_Position] [int]);
MERGE [Slides] USING (
VALUES (@p301, @p302, @p303, @p304, @p305, @p306, @p307, @p308, @p309, 0),
(@p310, @p311, @p312, @p313, @p314, @p315, @p316, @p317, @p318, 1),
